Please go to this thread to download the 10.0 system.  
<http://www.forexfactory.com/showthread.php?t=308304>  
In this thread we will talk about range trading with the 1H CTR BOTH EA. We will use the 4H CTR and Daily recovery EA for 2nd and 3rd level trades. I traded this system through the first week of August and the results were stunning. These are live trades using .03 and .05 cents lots. Here are my results:  
  
**Gross Profit:** **106.58** **Gross Loss:** **15.64** **Total Net Profit:** **90.94** The 90.94 was an incredible 8.8% increase in my account of 1035 dollars. That was trading .03 and .05 pennies lots. I cant really expect to do that every week but it sure was a nice start.  
  
_**Total for the month of August 2011= 22% of the account**_ post 147 pg. 10  
  
You can use the CTR EAs whenever range conditions are met or you can constantly range trade 24/7 while using just the low volatility currency pairs. See my excel sheet and use only the following pairs listed as volatility of 1-3. From two months experience I dropped a couple of pairs but these will be the ones I will use:  
  
  
aud/jpy, aud/nzd, aud/usd,   
cad/jpy, chf/jpy, eur/gbp,   
gbp/cad, gbp/usd, nzd,chf,   
nzd/jpy, usd/cad, usd/jpy  
  
That gives me a mix of aud-3 cad-3 chf-2 jpy-5 eur-1 gbp-3 nzd-3 usd-4  
  
I did not use nzd/usd to give me better balance, I chose all the #3 volatile pairs except aud/chf. Don’t trust the chf right now, it is not ranging very well. I chose two gbp because the gbp has been ranging very well the last two years. So until they stop ranging I am going to trade it. This list of pairs traded can be changed from time to time based on market volatility. For example if the GBP starts making headlines I will drop the gbp/cad and possibly the gbp/usd.

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41648_3.gif) nanningbob](nanningbob)

The aud/chf is my nightmare trade of the week. From the entrance at a support on the buy 1H to it finally reversed was -1400 pips. I have never tried to recover such a big number before. What saved me a lot of headaches was 10.0 kept me from having too many levels to recover from sooooooooooo ............. I have gotten back most of my deficit. My only losses in trading for the week is I closed 2 levels that I had entered violating my 10.0 recovery. If I had stuck with the basic 10.0 my 2nd level would have entered and I would be close to BE now. Instead I took a couple of losses covered by my profits and my recovery has brought me back 2/3 of BE. So instead of dealing with 4 or 5 trades and being patient I have done 10 trades of which 7 are winners 2 were losers and 1 loser trade left. Anyways I have almost finished recovery of a -1400 deficit (something I have never done before). I dont know if that is good news or bad news but one thing is certain. I wont be range trading aud/chf since with this latest move it has now become a category 4 currency pair. ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1)

Studying a currency's tendencies is also helpful in recovery but I knew the aud/chf has a V-turn tendency when it moves big. This is also helpful to know. Most trading gurus tell you about their successful trades. I think I learn more about trading to sometimes talk about the ugly ones. None have been more ugly than this. With the right lot size to account size you can survive these things.

  * [#20](/thread/post/4868659#post4868659 "Post Permalink")

  * Aug 15, 2011 3:23am  Aug 15, 2011 3:23am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41648_3.gif) nanningbob](nanningbob)

  * Joined Jun 2007 | Status: Teach men to fish | [7,384 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41648)

One last thing about recovery trades. Recovery trades and negative DD are simple interest trades. In other words they happen once and they are done, no compounding. Winning trades are compound interest. In other words profits continue to increase the account and each winning trade is like banking compound interest over a long period of time. Losing trades and DD are simple interest in that once they are done they no long continue to add to the loses. So as my DD grew and diminished in size, my winners kept increasing my account like compound interest does. My losing aud/chf trade did not keep growing but eventually lessened in size until it was closed with profits. In any case my account got bigger and my loser trade is gone and cant take away my profits anymore. My winning trades however, will keep being added to my account. I dont know if this makes sense to you but that is how I am beginning to look at it. My account keeps growing from my winners and my DD is like breathing in and out. It gets bigger, then smaller, then bigger then smaller but the bottom line keeps growing. I like that, but very complicated logic.

Can someone help clarify for me - I used the NB 5.0 counter trend system so maybe that is making me a bit confused.  
  
Rules  
If a candle high/low moves inbetween the daily MA's then we are in a pause of trend or start of renage trading and looking to use CTR system.  
  
Now with 4hr system are we now looking to ctr back into the prevailing trend ie if trend is down price action has now retraced back inbetween MA's on daily then we drill down to 4hr and look to sell using perhaps RWB multi indicator to show over brought   
  
Or as we are now in range we just trade like the old NB5.0 and trade up and down as dictated by RBW indicators  
  
In 1 hr CTR do the same but on low volitile pairs (trade both ways ) or again are we looking to get back in on trend ?

  * [#32](/thread/post/4871418#post4871418 "Post Permalink")

  * Aug 16, 2011 12:44am  Aug 16, 2011 12:44am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41648_3.gif) nanningbob](nanningbob)

  * Joined Jun 2007 | Status: Teach men to fish | [7,384 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41648)

This is the strength of 1H CTR. It knocks down a lot of trades on low volatility pairs. Since Aug. 1, and this is a live account, it has taken161 closed trades. 133 are winners 28 losers for a win percentage of 82.6% During that time I suffered some of the biggest moves in Forex since Oct. 2008. aud/chf -1400, gbp/cad -780, nzd/chf -800, were some of my DD. Despite that 10.0 kept me from entering too often and having too many levels. I waited patiently for my reentry and tried not to guess at it. Each one, except for the gbp/cad so far, came back and broke even or even made a nice profit. I have an incredible 13% increase of my original amount profit through today. Yet I am trading 3 penny or 5 penny trades. Why is this working. With 3 penny trades I only need 35 pips to make a dollar, 70 pips to make two dollars, and 100 pips to make 3 dollars on most currencies. Multiply that times 133 winners and you can see the money add up fast but the DD are comparatively small. I cant tell you how tickled I am at these numbers. If I can knock that down in what is really a horrible month for range trading, just imagine what will happen if prices do range. I mean I invented a trend system and a counter trend system to go with 10.0 but if this keeps up, why bother. I have my money maker.  
  
Lets do the math. aud/chf -1400 x .03 = 42.00 dollars down at one point. With 1000 in the bank that is easy to handle. 133 winners at 1.69 average win = 224.77 then subtract a small handful of losers and you can see where this is going. The DD breathes in and out, in and out, but the winners just keep adding to the pile. This is really exciting to me. This is like comparing compound interest to simple interest. The winners keep compounding, the losers are a one time event.   
  
Well time for bed. Oh that is why I use 10-15 currencies to trade. While a couple are running away from you the rest are piling on the profit.

> 
> Ignored

Thank you for your note. I dont know why but FOREX seems to be a different animal when it comes to trading rules. I finally believed them to be mostly garbage.   
  
1\. For example, you are told to trade one currency and get to know it, yet almost all investor advice I have heard, read, or seen tells you to diversify your portfolio. Trading many currencies, if you choose a good mix, allows for that.   
  
2\. You are told to have tight SL yet I have never heard of a broker advise a client to put in a trade with 1/8 of a penny stop on a stock trade. Yet that is what is done in Forex. 30 pip stop is 3/10 of a penny. I dont know anyone who trades like this with stocks, futures, bonds, commodities, on and on.   
  
3\. You are told to never do multiple levels or trades, (I don't mean martingale either) Yet it is common practice in stocks, etc. to add to your position over time and increase your holdings. Buy and hold is the watchword of the stock market. The big boys who trade with millions on the line buy and hold and add to their positions over time.   
  
I really didnt become profitable in Forex until I threw out practically every piece of advice I ever got from so called Forex gurus. I think they just try to sell the rehashed garbage of everyone else. If you think about it, a lot of what I teach is based on Non Forex investment strategy. Start small, add to your position over time, diversify, and give your trade space and time to move in your direction. That is basic stock strategy 101. What is a stock purchase plan at almost every company in the world? Set aside part of your paycheck every month and buy their stock and hold until your retire. What do I do? I buy at a price. If it works I close and make profit, if it doesnt at some point I buy again, and sometimes I buy again and then I follow the rule that is 100% true all the time in FOREX. What goes down must come up and what goes up must come down. Time is always on your side if you trade with some smarts and patience.

I am using it differently. Started the CTR BOTH EA Sunday evening on 15 pairs, H1 TF with MPTM BE 40 pips and BE Profit of 30 pips, no TP but moving the SL up every 10 pips. It is running on automatic ever since (have not had cause to intervene) and the results have been astonishing. Using 20 cents per trade the profit thus far is $240 and floating DD is $70.   
  
As far the volatility of the pairs are concerned I use mataf indicator and just to give you a rough idea of the recent wild fluctuations, the average daily pip movement for the very stable USDJPY was.  
last 10 weeks 71.4 pips  
last 5 weeks 83.8 pips  
last 2 weeks 98.9 pips  
last week 60 pips.  
  
The fluctuations of some other pairs jumped from around 200 to over 400 pips!

Hi Mike  
It is not an indicator for mt4, but a utility provided by mataf, you can find it here <http://www.forexticket.co.uk/en/tools/02-01-volatility> .  
  
Bob`s spread sheet is excellent, however, if you wish to see volatility over short periods this will do the job. For instance you can see the jump in the volatility of EURCHF.  
Kind regards

Thus far none. This EA is very neat, at 08:31 open a buy GBPUSD, closed at 11:51 with 101 pips profit. At 11:53 opened a sell GBPUSD, now it is -82 pips loss. So thus far there is no need for recovery. One thing I learned in using recovery is that if you use it often for trades which are around 100 pips down there is a danger of a huge DD when you have a long run of 400 to 600 pips which are very common these says.

Dear Flame (please feel free to tell me to go to hell on this one)  
  
Ok i am testing my recovery system based on my ideas and bobs input and wondered if you could help modify the dash board to allow this more easily  
  
**_Recovery System_**  
A trade goes in dd by 100pips at that momment i hedge it (I obviously do this manually and have missed a couple so have 123, 111 being hedged at the moment.)   
  
The trade does its hedge untill it travels out of the bands (no mod required here just watch Out indicator on your dashboard)  
  
Once out of daily ma-lines set recovery ea4 on so as soon as it crosses back into ma bands it will add the new recovery trade- if all goes well and recovery makes up the 100pip deficit close all at BE or profit what ever basket is set at as per dashboard.  
  
My difficulty is   
1) setting the hedge manually it would be great if auto option was available for this _but wondered if you could add hedge at x pips (this being a user defined variable you can set)  
  
2) Also and this is asking a bit and out of the scope of the dashboard but it would be great if once outside mabands ea 4 recovery kicks in assuming hedge is on (This is more a request for Steve to consider in his EA design)  
  
If the first could be done it would be great if not well you don't get anything with out asking and at least i asked - Bob perhaps you could review this and add your 2 penny worht  
  
thnaks

  * Aug 19, 2011 6:42pm  Aug 19, 2011 6:42pm 

  * [ astral77](astral77)

  * | Joined Nov 2009  | Status: Trader | [1,196 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=122957)

> [Quoting eltax100](/thread/post/4884086#post4884086 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> I have set up 2 demo accounts one for CTR and Trend look forward to contributing, only wish i could code.
> 
> Ignored

Hi  
  
1H CTR Both EA is loaded on individual charts to trigger trades. Mptm can be loaded on any chart and you can set it to manage ALL trades or some trades according to various criteria. You can have two different EAs on two charts of the same pair as long as they have different magic numbers so they know which trade belongs to which EA. However, this is not advisable since it may lead to complications. Having said that it is ok to have a EA plus mptm, since mptm is a trade management EA and does not trigger trades by itself.  
  
I hope this makes sense.  
  
Kind Regards 

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

  * [ astral77](astral77)

How is everyone getting along? So far the EA has been a dream. OK, during the last 36 hours the DD has shot up but it is still well within the acceptable range (less than 5%). It is very strange for me since I have been used to trading Bob`s system manually and now this fully automatic EA is doing all the work and I am a spectator.  
  
One thing that we have to be very careful is the recovery and hedge. Always bear in mind Bob`s golden rule "What goes up must come down". It is very tempting to start recovery at -100 pip and in all probability we will recover a lot of trades doing so. However, when we get a 600 or even 800 pip move without a decent retrace, then it becomes an account threatening martingale situation. So caution, practice and experience are of utmost importance. If or when we can truly master the art of recovery trading then we can enjoy very successful trading experience.   
  
Kind regards  
P.S. my latest set file for mptm is attached, mind you I will most probably switch to FLAME`s fantastic adaptation of phover dashboard to manage the trades.

The 1H EA does close when it reaches the opposite band. I have that in for my protection because i am away from my computer a lot and want the TP. I will post EAs without the Close this weekend using Steve's EAs with the one time entrance and you have to reset to work again. I originally didnt think of the situation where they would close as a negative because they had been running a while as DD. I will correct that and post the changes later. So yes that is how the EAs work. Sorry if I didnt make that clear enough in my booklets.

Fantastic my friend, well done and keep up the good work. Bob`s system has been proven to be successful over two years of live account testing (please see Ver5 thread). However, the main problem we faced up to now was the floating DD. Scoobs told us some time ago as to what is acceptable DD for the professional traders and it was less than 5%. So we want to be in the same position as professionals. Indeed that is the main reason BOB created version 10.   
  
IMHO your capital to lot size ratio can be problematic. We have almost come to conclusion that for safe trading of this system for lot size of 10 cents you would need an account balance of $2000. At present the markets are very kind to the system and there is no problem, however, you should be ready when the markets are not as cooperative.  
  
Moreover, recovery which is Bob`s fantastic and unique invention is very subjective and requires plenty of practice, discretion and correct trader psychology. Unfortunately, over the last two years I have seen some very competent traders becoming unstuck on this and they left FF disappointed and disillusioned. This is a great shame because a number of them were much more experienced and competent than I. Therefore, I strongly urge anyone new to Bob`s system to go through his past posts and thoroughly read EVERYTHING he has written (which is quite extensive) on this subject. Believe me it will make hell of a lot of difference (i.e. between success and failure).  
  
Kind Regards

  * [#83](/thread/post/4886115#post4886115 "Post Permalink")

  * Aug 20, 2011 8:59am  Aug 20, 2011 8:59am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41648_3.gif) nanningbob](nanningbob)

  * Joined Jun 2007 | Status: Teach men to fish | [7,384 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41648)

OK another decent week. Increased the account 3.94% so that is very acceptable. I will increase my lot size by one penny starting Monday so instead of trading .03 and .05 I will go to .04 and .06 2nd level. Remember that is pennies not dimes make sure you all understand the difference on that. I am up 17.2% for the month from my original starting amount of funds.   
  
If you wish to figure percent of increase you take your starting balance lets say it is 1000 dollars. You increase it 172 dollars so your present balance is 1172. You compare your increase to the original balance so you take 172 and divide it by 1000 and you get .172 or 17.2%. 172/1000=0.172 That would be by the month.  
  
Lets say you wanted to do the last week and you made 50 dollars. You would take your balance of 1172 subtract 50 dollars to get your starting balance for the week which is 1122. So 50 divided by 1122 is 0.0445 or 4.45%. So that is how it is done. Account is up 17.2% for the month and 4.45% for the week. ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1)  
  
Now here is the exciting part. If you follow my formula of increasing lot size one penny every 200 dollars earned and you can average 20% a month. At the end of 1 year you have 8916.00 dollars in the account or a 791.6% increase of your account. Lets throw in a couple losing months so you average 10% a month (yes it will happen guys) you will have 3,138 dollars in your account or a 213.8% increase for you account. Now I believe that is slightly better than a bank. ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1) ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1) ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1)

When ever they break outside the norm. For example OCT. 2008 changed everything concerning volatility. The markets are far more volatile the last 3 years as compared to the 10 years before that. The eur/chf used to be one of the least volatile pairs, well now it is not since the Greek thing broke out last year. Eur/gbp has been a great non volatile pair but I think that will change if the Euro breaks up. aud/nzd used to be the best ranging pair until China started buying everything up it can find in Australia. Markets change, people keep predicting doom and gloom for the USA but it still remains the strongest economy in the world and against many currencies it has appreciated the last 3 years instead of spiraling into hyper-inflation. So these things can change and when they do we will change. Right now the Eur/usd is ranging nicely and giving me several good trades a week. That will end soon enough though/  
  
  
I used to have this beautiful EA called the 100x40 which made me some good money but it is worthless now because of the volatility issue. 10.0, I hope, is my final answer to this volatile market.

Not the AUD/NZD, It used to bounce 30-60 pips up and down every 5-10 minutes and you could make a killing on it even with the 15-20 pip [spreads](/brokers/spreads "View Live Spreads on the Broker Guide") back then. Now it moves more like normal currency pairs. Get China out of the way and you probably could.   
  
Aud/cad hmmmmmmmmmmm dont know havent looked at that one. maybe with the 10.0 sytem as a backup if things went bad you could. I looked at the chart on aud/cad and on 8-2 and 8-8 it would have gone outside the range of that EA. The run up in mid March to end of April would probably have done in that EA also. So you would have periods of recovery at times. Whether this would overcome its profits I dont know. I do know it doesnt bounce up and down like the aud/nzd used to do. That thing would spike 60 pips 2-5 times every hour and I would pick off the tops and bottoms. Best kept secret in Forex but it doesnt do that anymore. I did use it on the usd/sig (singapore dollar) successfully but that is no longer offered. USD/HKD might work too but I cant trade that one either. I tried the Danish Kroner ?? and Euro but the spread widens too much when it spikes for it to work. Any currency that is tied to another like the RMB is to the USD and is not free floating it would work. For example if we could do the RMB because it stays very stable and not move would probably be a big money maker if it was trade able.

  * Aug 23, 2011 2:29pm  Aug 23, 2011 2:29pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar82380_5.gif) whitegoodman](whitegoodman)

  * | Joined Oct 2008  | Status: Trader | [1,080 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=82380)

really enjoying just using the 1hr CTR both ways EA. I think using that as a substitute for original 60x90 'idea' is working quite well for me atm. A couple of thoughts:  
  
\- despite some people having problem when trades close when it hit the other BB at a loss, i think this is a good risk mitigation thing and often gets you back in the direction for a profitable trade on the next entry. You are getting more losing trades then just averaging and using recovery but the DD is SIGNIFICANTLY less I believe and the winners still outweigh the losers in both win % and pips.  
  
\- an idea for adapting the EA for re-entries. Is it possible to set rules like price has to go 'x' amount of pips into drawdown from the first entry and also having the MA cross the BB (same entry rules) to reopen a second trade at a lot size that is 'x' multiplier. The rules on closing trades when hitting the other BB still apply for controlling risk. I think this would work well when you get price running up a BB, then it pauses and is say for eg 150pips in DD, then it spikes again to cross the BB then reverses in the direction of original entry.  
  
thoughts? 

Grabbing the bull by the horns!

  * [#107](/thread/post/4895032#post4895032 "Post Permalink")

  * Aug 24, 2011 3:44am  Aug 24, 2011 3:44am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar185500_2.gif) George Adams](george*adams)

  * | Joined Jul 2011  | Status: Investor & Trader | [138 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=185500)

> [Quoting peje](/thread/post/4892965#post4892965 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> Hello,  
>    
>  though I have studied booklets I am confused about proper using of EA for recovery.  
>  I use '10.0 1H CTR BOTH' on GBPUSD. Buy trade was sent some days ago. Yeasterday I decided to replace this EA by 10.0 DAILY RECOVERY after -125 pips expecting to send another buy trade but EA sent sell trade. Could someone advise how to use EA just for recovery?
> 
> Ignored

I will explain to you what I do and use a current recovery of the EUR/CAD, which is being a bit difficult right now. The first point I will make is if you are going to trade this system make sure you are not over leveraging your account on the initial trade or having too many recovery positions open. Managing DD is a big part in making the system profitable. This pair can move 10,000 pips and I am still ok - not happy, but ok with my account. On to the trade, you will see on the below chart where my initial CTR trade entry, which was 1.3773 @ .03 (L1). After I took the trade in early August, you see the run up when commodities currencies really fell off. When it does this, the beauty about the recovery system is you just wait until it completes its run and begins to pull back to the blue line (2MA). The way the daily recovery EA works is it trades "outside - in" (OI) on the chart. So, when the price comes back to the blue line and touches, it enters, anticipating a move back to the red line or beyond. 6 days later my second (L2) trade enters at 1.4031 @ .05 (green circle) and does not retrace much and heads back up to the 1.4200 area. Now, one could look back and say why did you not take L2 at 1.4250? The issue there is you don't know if the run is over at that point. It could easily continued to 1.45, so the definition that the run is over is coming back to the blue line. It is tempting, but in my experience, an entry like that is purely a guess and usually ends up being a poor one. After the green circle, it is heading back up and 5 days later it gets to the purple circle. At that point it would have entered at around 1.4150 and again gives us a head fake and does not retrace much. The purple circle explains one of the rules I use in recovery, which is I like to see space of around 200 pips (at least), before taking another position. So, if I would have entered at that point, my breakeven point would not have been affected much for the retracement. Good thing I did not enter because it headed up higher. The last two days, I did have good spacing for L3, so I had the EA loaded and it just missed entry, which is ok with me, I will just wait. So, I am 18 days into this one, patiently waiting for the L3 level to enter and my current BE point is 1.3934 (L1 + L2).   
  
I will update you as this one progresses to show the next entry and completion of the recovery. If this one really starts to get nasty, I will also share at that time other strategies I have used in the past to aid in removing the DD. Keys with recovery is to be patient on the daily chart and keep good spacing on your L2 and L3 trades, waiting for Bob's golden rule to kick in - what goes up, must come down.  
  
Hope that helps.  
  
George

> Hello George,  
>  thank you for explanation, logic of a trade sending seems to be clear. > Ignored

Peje, I am trying to understand your chart and not sure I am following it correctly, so I will interprete it based on some assumptions. Let me know if they are not correct. It looks like you had a BUY order first on the GBP/USD, which was well above the blue line, perhaps trying to re-enter the uptrend. The pair then drops down the to blue line (and you have the daily recovery EA on), once it touches the blue line, it looks like that is about the area which you have your sell order. If this is your scenario, then the EA performed correctly. With the daily recovery EA, it works outside-in, so (coming from the outside of the red and blue lines) the blue line creates a sell order and the red line sends a buy order. So, you are anticipating a move to go in between the red and blue lines for recovery. If I was in your position there, I would have looked to use probably the 4H CTR Buy EA to try and recover the trade, once it moved towards the -200 pip range. You are correct, if the L2 entered as a buy, judging from the candle, you would have been able to recover.  
  
Hope that helps...  
  
George

I know the implications are the need for much larger a/c balance but with the profits ver 10.0 is making at present the returns will still be quite reasonable.

I am based in the US and the above as listed by Astral77 is how I am set-up. I have one account which is for Trend trading. A second account which is for range/CTR. The pairs listed for each account do not cross over and are specific for the trading style. So, if I felt the need to hedge, an available pair in the other account is always available for that purpose. I have been fortunate enough that I don't hedge much at all to reduce DD with the 10.0 system. It is a pain sometimes switching between systems/brokers (I use two different brokers for the accounts), but it does provide good flexibility.  
  
Good trading to all..  
  
George

> Disliked
> 
> really enjoying just using the 1hr CTR both ways EA. I think using that as a substitute for original 60x90 'idea' is working quite well for me atm. A couple of thoughts:  
>    
>  \- despite some people having problem when trades close when it hit the other BB at a loss, i think this is a good risk mitigation thing and often gets you back in the direction for a profitable trade on the next entry. You are getting more losing trades then just averaging and using recovery but the DD is SIGNIFICANTLY less I believe and the winners still outweigh the losers in both win % and pips.  
>    
>  \- an idea for adapting the EA for re-entries. Is it possible to set rules like price has to go 'x' amount of pips into drawdown from the first entry and also having the MA cross the BB (same entry rules) to reopen a second trade at a lot size that is 'x' multiplier. The rules on closing trades when hitting the other BB still apply for controlling risk. I think this would work well when you get price running up a BB, then it pauses and is say for eg 150pips in DD, then it spikes again to cross the BB then reverses in the direction of original entry.
> 
> Ignored

bump this.. thoughts bob?  
  
anyone know if this is difficult to code in?

Hello nanning..What would be your advise to people who don't want to use the EA but rather trade manually? Also can you confirm if I am following you clearly:  
After getting a confirmation from the daily chart (I only trade range, not trend), I go to the 1 hour chart and look for signals. (both stoch lines above-below the 90-10 lines, price hits outer BB bands). Then I enter the trade with 1 lot. If it goes against me 100 pips, I go to Level 2 with the same lot and same direction. Another 100 pips against me I enter my last lot which is 3.  
I know every detail is written but there is so much information I came to a point where I am confused.

  * [#123](/thread/post/4898093#post4898093 "Post Permalink")

  * Aug 24, 2011 11:19pm  Aug 24, 2011 11:19pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41648_3.gif) nanningbob](nanningbob)

  * Joined Jun 2007 | Status: Teach men to fish | [7,384 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41648)

> [Quoting The7](/thread/post/4898058#post4898058 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> Hello nanning..What would be your advise to people who don't want to use the EA but rather trade manually? Also can you confirm if I am following you clearly:  
>  After getting a confirmation from the daily chart (I only trade range, not trend), I go to the 1 hour chart and look for signals. (both stoch lines above-below the 90-10 lines, price hits outer BB bands). Then I enter the trade with 1 lot. If it goes against me 100 pips, I go to Level 2 with the same lot and same direction. Another 100 pips against me I enter my last lot which is 3.  
>  I know...
> 
> Ignored

Reentering every 100 pips is dangerous. A good run and you have some pretty stiff negatives to overcome. Better to use 200 or more, but 10.0 you reenter when it crosses back on the Daily thereby giving you a better chance without a run against you and getting better separation between trades. Yes you understand the 1.1.3 formula which is my favorite formula in recovery. However, if the distance is great between levels, then I might go 1,2,3 or 1,2,4  
  
If you are going to manually trade then use some kind of warning system. It lets you know there is a cross in price so you can check on it. 

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

  * [#125](/thread/post/4898648#post4898648 "Post Permalink")

  * Aug 25, 2011 1:32am  Aug 25, 2011 1:32am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar185500_2.gif) George Adams](george*adams)

  * | Joined Jul 2011  | Status: Investor & Trader | [138 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=185500)

> [Quoting yaniv_av](/thread/post/4897184#post4897184 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> Hi George,  
>    
>  Thanks for this explanation. Although, I think I missed something very basic here - as far as I understood from nanningbob's booklets, the heart of 10.0 is that when the market changes behavior (based on daily chart) - we must change immediately our trading style to the new behavior. Meaning, if the market was ranging, but now switched to UT, we should stop range trading and start trend trading. it stated many times by nanningbob in his booklets.   
>  So my question is simple - as the euraud changed to UP, why trying to recover instead...
> 
> Ignored

I think that depends on your trading style and whether or not you choose to use stop losses. Personally, I am a counter trend trader and I choose not to use SL's and recover. I am a below average trend trader and it comes difficult for me, however with the 10.0 philosophy I am working on improving that. That philosophy you mention above I follow prior to entry. Once I am in a trade, based on my selection of recovery vs. stop loss, it is BE or profit, then move on to the next set-up. (at least a very large percentage of the time).   
  
Let me show you what I have difficulty with on trend trading and applying what you suggested above. Below is the 1h chart of the EUR/CAD starting on Aug 3-10. So, there I am sitting at 1.3773 and the pair is just consolidating around that level. The green circle is where I was asleep at the wheel and for a brief moment this pair went 50 pips into profit. (probably one reason I need to test out MPTM, which I have not used in the past). Then, on August 4 at the blue box, you see where this pair takes off on a 400 pip run and the recovery process has begun. The area I really stuggled with these trending trades (after I was in and decided to change directions) is where do you enter and where do you put the stop loss and shift gears. I was very poor at this and a vast majority of the time, it would come back on me. So, it seemed like I was always on the wrong side of the trade. I am sure there are traders who are very good at this, combining it with fundamentals and get it right most of the time. I like Bob's method of looking at trend vs. counter trend, prior to entry and trading that way through exit.   
  
Also, you mentioned the buy EA after using the SL. It would not have entered during the uptrend of Aug 4, so you would have been looking at entering around the 1.4000 level on Aug 8, if the 1H Buy was used.  
  
I hope that makes sense....  
  
Best of trading to you.   
  
George 

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

Yes Yes Yes.  
What you said above is correct! Thanks for the reply. I do like to note about some of your trading philosophy though. I couldnt agree more,you had said a profit banked in wouldnt hurt/keeps the bank at bay something like that? Breath in breath out comment? I had unconsciously used that very same thing you tought in about a 2 - 3 months experiment in a small account, guess what it,has grown >20 percent since.Profits are banked in ,even in deep drawdown, what happened was when the prices kept trending the profit are banked in ,kinda hedged. Positions are reloaded(breath in ,breath out) and before long the drawdown disappeared.  
The price came back to close in overall profits! All that using micro/ nanolots using a single pair. I thought about your pdf's and manuals , it is about the same thing that i did! The idea must have merits after all. I just had to know the long term direction and thats it.  
In my opinion, the key that allowed the experiment to survive is to keep booking those profits and reloading position. Thats the crucial step to overcome drawdown during that period.Not forgetting diversification,multiple level/ trades even when trading 1 or 2 pairs. Note that I also did hedge both ways long/short so cannot use this in criminals brooker.  
Things that you said are not taught anywhere in the web, so i consider your philosophy ,ideas, thoughts as gold! even though i didnt trade your system it feels very similar.Very helpful and provided me with insight. You could even construct many systems using your ideas alone, its not that difficult but also simple.  
Thank you again,it feels like i had been reinforced knowing youre not alone trading this kind of stuffs.

  * [#131](/thread/post/4900926#post4900926 "Post Permalink")

  * Aug 25, 2011 6:14pm  Aug 25, 2011 6:14pm 

  * [ censura](censura)

  * | Joined Sep 2006  | Status: Trader | [405 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=17875)

I tade NB10 ctr on 1hr timeframe as per NB rules and template  
  
I have a tp of 40 pips   
  
I have NO Stop Loss - (This will kill your account)  
  
  
  
I traded NB5 for 1 year and made money from it - My issue was always the scalling of positions level 2 , l3 etc 1.1.2.4 step  
  
When to get in to l2 l3 etc i tried MA 200, 500 i tried fixed 200 , 500 etc but could not decide on what was best and i didnt work for me   
  
After a lot of thought and trys i have decided on   
If a trade goes to -100 pips i place a counter trade to the same value  
(currently 0.02 lot size) to hedge / Fix my dd  
  
I then match out the losses ie the 2 pairs with winners eg  
  
On Monday i had GBPNZD go bad on me for -100 i hedged it fixed at about $18 loss i then waited until winners came along to close and match the trade i didnt have towait long here an hour later GBPCAD trade and CADJPY trade winners which gave me $18 profit so then clossed the GBPNZD 2 trades the first and the hedge.  
  
To my mind this is simple alot less risk and alot less worry. Obviously you need more winners than losers but the system is doing this.   
  
Cautionary Note - My account is over leaveraged (i explained this before)  
I had trades set at 0.02 by mistake rather than 0.01 this has meant at one point i was 24% in dd When i go live on 5th Sept i will use 0.01 lot size for each $1,000 , this would effectivly have halved my returns on my demo account which is what i am reporting on.   
  
Also the markets are ranging ok and i have not encountered a huge trend break out . My hope is that i can add an automatic hedge function into the ea bob had produced with variable hedge_at as a user defined parameter. I am not a coader so doing so learning to see if i can ammend the ctr to suit. (Obviously if there are coders out there who can do this great)  
  
Hope this helps

Good strategy but my idea would be to hang onto the trade until you get the recovery cross of the 2MA. close the profit trade and counter with equal pips. 50 pips later the loss trade is breakeven. You then can ride it further to see if you can make a profit on the trade. In other words you are looking for a 50 pip retracement. ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1) I cant hedge so dont know, but I bet I could do it.   
  
Also you may really want to consider doing any buys on Euros. See article below, a bit sensational but the basic truth behind it does exist.   
  
[http://www.forexfactory.com/news.php?do=news&id=311347](http://www.forexfactory.com/news.php?do=news&id=311347)

  * [ Ckp](ckp)

Hi Bob. An observation. When using 10.0 H1 CTR BOTH on a H1 chart you definitely want to wacth out for extremely quiet periods lasting longer than 8-12 hours at a time. The BB narrows as a result and the trade could enter much sooner than you might expect. See attached. GBPUSD in the last 24 hrs. Best you can do here is suppose is remove the EA until volume returns... Any thoughts on that?

Today was a difficult day i have had 6 x -100 hedge trades to close out with winners and thus the day stands at +1.63 % dd is 5,24%  
  
Total to date since Monday 22nd - 102.52%  
  
I have 1 more hedge to close out awating corresponding winners to allow me to do this.  
  
I try and do this as quickly as possible as there is the opportunity cost of having a pair fixed in a hedge ie i cant get any winners from it while it sits there.  
  
So was today a success ! i believe so as there are going to be 20% of the trading days when the mkt trends and if i can break even or even have to take a small loss it does not matter in the grand scheme of things  
  
take care and keep trading

  * [#142](/thread/post/4904510#post4904510 "Post Permalink")

  * Aug 26, 2011 6:30pm  Aug 26, 2011 6:30pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41648_3.gif) nanningbob](nanningbob)

  * Joined Jun 2007 | Status: Teach men to fish | [7,384 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41648)

> [Quoting peje](/thread/post/4904157#post4904157 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> Hello,  
>    
>  What is your experience with MPTM 25+10? MPTM closes my recovery trade based on settings as it goes in my favour and let the first one in loss. Both trades together were far from BE. MPTM manages trades individualy even more position of a pair opened.  
>  How to manage recovery if I want to yous MPTM on other pairs?
> 
> Ignored

You dont use MPTM for recovery trades. OR You set the MPTM to handle trades by magic number. So set all your 1st entry EAs to one magic number and use a MPTM for it set at that number. And then set your recovery trades at another magic number and set your MPTM to manage those EAs at that magic number.   
  
The code is below:  
  
extern string ManagementStyle="You can select more than one option";  
extern bool ManageByMagicNumber=false;  
extern int MagicNumber=1; set to true and change magic number  
extern bool ManageByTradeComment=false;  
extern string TradeComment = "Fib";  
extern bool ManageByTickeNumber=false;  
extern int TicketNumber;  
extern string OverRide="ManageThisPairOnly will override all previous";  
extern string OverRide2="or can be used in combination with 1 of above";  
extern bool ManageThisPairOnly=false;  
extern bool ManageSpecifiedPairs=false;//############## ADDED BY CACUS  
extern string PairsToManage="AUDJPY,AUDUSD,CHFJPY,EURCHF,EURGBP,EURJPY,EURUSD,GBPCHF,GBPJPY,GBPUSD,NZDJPY,NZDUSD,USDCHF,USDJPY";//############## ADDED BY CACUS  
// This allows the ea to manage all existing trades  
extern string OverRide1="ManageAllTrades will override all others";  
extern bool ManageAllTrades=true;Set to False  
extern bool ManagingNanningbobTrades=false;  
  
When done making changes make sure you hit the compile button OR save with a new name and hit compile button.

  * [#143](/thread/post/4905958#post4905958 "Post Permalink")

  * Aug 27, 2011 12:28am  Aug 27, 2011 12:28am

  * [ Frodog](frodog)

Hi Censura I have been using mptm to hedge at 100. It works well and you don't need to be at your computer. The trouble with hedging is when price moves 100 pips then hedge trade is taken, then price retraces back to original entry. So your left with original entry in profit and hedge trade at -100 or more. This happened to me on cad/jpy

  * [#148](/thread/post/4907142#post4907142 "Post Permalink")

  * Aug 27, 2011 1:29pm  Aug 27, 2011 1:29pm 

  * [ Frodog](frodog)

  * | Joined Jun 2009  | Status: Trader | [104 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=106966)

I really like the way this 1hr ctr rakes in the pips. It's a very active ea that takes full advantage of ranging times.   
  
I have found closing at market closing/opening times as Bob does to be very profitable. I have found more often than not the market retraces at the start of new session. Also using the sto, and the middle bb line for TP works well for me. I would not have made as much profit if I waited for price to reach opposite BB before closing.   
  
I like Bobs call of not trying to hit a home run on each trade, but rather take smaller profits more often.

> [Quoting nanningbob](/thread/post/4904510#post4904510 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> You dont use MPTM for recovery trades. OR You set the MPTM to handle trades by magic number. So set all your 1st entry EAs to one magic number and use a MPTM for it set at that number. And then set your recovery trades at another magic number and set your MPTM to manage those EAs at that magic number.   
>    
>  The code is below:  
>    
>  extern string ManagementStyle="You can select more than one option";
> 
> Ignored

Thank you for reply. This is exactly what I start to do. MPTM manages just first trades based on magic number and I manually enter the same TP for first and recovery trade on BE plus small profit.  
This is what I expected from MPTM but there seems to be no solution for such case, possible basket trades but these are managed again based on magic number which is different for first and recovery trade so it is not usable as well as trade comment.

  * [#151](/thread/post/4908241#post4908241 "Post Permalink")

  * Aug 29, 2011 12:58am  Aug 29, 2011 12:58am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar185500_2.gif) George Adams](george*adams)

  * | Joined Jul 2011  | Status: Investor & Trader | [138 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=185500)

Thought I would update the recovery of this pair as Thursday brought some decisions to consider and Friday was a roller coaster ride. The pair seems to still be defying gravity, but I like it and I believe this week might be the week to get move down to the BE point. So, I am in at 1.4231 with L3 and Thursday looks to be a good day moving my direction and my BE is at 1.4080. Below is the 1H chart to show the move and some decisions to consider. At the left of the chart you see the blue circle which shows some resistance around 1.4140. At that moment in time when we see the pair dropping to this range, there were two options (not including hedging or changing our direction, but remaining in recovery trend short). First, the L3 trade was profitable enough to BE with the L2 trade at 1.4045. So, we could have done that with the assumption the pair would not break 1.4140 to our BE point, then look to re-enter higher perhaps with the 1h CTR with an L2 trade and again raise our BE point without increasing our exposure. It is always nice to get the recovery on the first move, but sometimes you have to piece it together or wait a little longer. The only risk with this option is it does break 1.4140 and you have your L1 trade still there, where if you would have been patient you would be out. However, with removing L2 and L3 your overall risk / exposure is lower. Second, which for this example I chose to do, was just remain patient looking for the next couple days to continue back down to 1.4080. On the next chart, I will show you a couple reasons why I like the position.  
  
George

  * Aug 29, 2011 1:22am  Aug 29, 2011 1:22am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar185500_2.gif) George Adams](george*adams)

  * | Joined Jul 2011  | Status: Investor & Trader | [138 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=185500)

The reason I chose to remain patient was two reasons. First, the EURO fundamentals I believe are to the downside. Second, the daily chart. If you look at the chart, to the upper left, it has serious resistance at the 1.4350 range. Actually, there is another candle you cannot see further to the left failing at 1.4350 as well. So, there is a nice ceiling there. If you see the green circle we have had 6 days of spinning tops and doji's which typically represents a reversal coming. This pair certainly can move above 1.4400 and if so, then some more creative strategies will need to be employed to remove DD, but I feel the probabilities are in our favor to hit 1.4080 before we close above 1.4400. If fundamentals where different or a stronger long term trend, then definitely would have taken option 1 from prior post and pieced this recovery together. Hope this is insightful for folks who have questions about recovery. Sometimes it is frustrating as it is with this pair...  
  
George

  * [#153](/thread/post/4913671#post4913671 "Post Permalink")

  * Aug 31, 2011 12:20am  Aug 31, 2011 12:20am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar185500_2.gif) George Adams](george*adams)

  * | Joined Jul 2011  | Status: Investor & Trader | [138 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=185500)

The EUR/CAD today hit our BE target of 1.4080 and closed out the L1, L2 and L3 trades. I hope that example was helpful to those who had questions about recovery and how I use it. In summary, the recovery took 22 trading days to complete and that is where the daily chart helps you to be patient with your L2 and L3 trades. Also, the rule of "in the range of 200 pips or more" for the next position helps keep your L2 and L3 trades effective in raising your BE level.   
  
As you saw in the last post there are a few different ways to remove DD and decisions to make as price moves your way, however this was strictly by the book on waiting for it to return to the blue line for entries and just being patient.   
  
Best of trading to all...  
  
George

  * [ jmw1970](jmw1970)

Hi All  
  
I am currently writing a multi-pair trader for the 1Hr CTR EA's as I am having difficulty with the number of charts open on my laptop  
  
This is in testing so far but produces a screen similar to below:-  
  
I will upload it to the thread once testing is complete.  
  
I have taken the logic directly from the original 1h CTR ea's  
  
I have noticed though that the logic for Buy is MA Low below Lower Band and the Bid less than the Lower Band (reversed for sell), this causes orders to be opened when the price may be on a run in the opposite direction, ie. price is going down and hugging the bollinger lower band the EA will open a buy  
  
Have I just been unlucky in that all my testing I keep on hitting these runs and hence running up big losses (well not actual losses because I am hedging them at -100 pips to deal with later)  
  
Would it not make sense to have the logic for buy to be MA Low is ABOVE Lower Band and the previous MA Low was BELOW the Lower band - ie. to ensure that the price is at least going at least towards the Upper band  
  
or is it that these odd runs are compensated by the winners and the fact the original method gives a better price entry  
  
Regards, John

  * [#160](/thread/post/4924826#post4924826 "Post Permalink")

  * Sep 3, 2011 8:01am  Sep 3, 2011 8:01am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41648_3.gif) nanningbob](nanningbob)

  * Joined Jun 2007 | Status: Teach men to fish | [7,384 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41648)

> [Quoting jmw1970](/thread/post/4924273#post4924273 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> Hi All  
>    
>  I am currently writing a multi-pair trader for the 1Hr CTR EA's as I am having difficulty with the number of charts open on my laptop  
>    
>  This is in testing so far but produces a screen similar to below:-  
>    
>  I will upload it to the thread once testing is complete.  
>    
>  I have taken the logic directly from the original 1h CTR ea's  
>    
>  I have noticed though that the logic for Buy is MA Low below Lower Band and the Bid less than the Lower Band (reversed for sell), this causes orders to be opened when the price may be on a run in the opposite direction,...
> 
> Ignored

Not a bad idea with the multi trader. Runs are a normal activity in Forex, there is no avoiding them. You choose to use hedging and stop losses, I choose to counter trade. I prefer counter trading and recovery trades. To each persons system are pluses and minuses. 10.0 was given to make recovery trades simpler and easier to do. I think hedging until the daily chart gives you the signal counter trade is a good idea. Hedging to wait until you have winners will have its drawbacks, I think, when the markets go trending this fall. You could have a news story that makes every trade hedge. You then dont have any pairs to profit yourself out of your hedges. However, if you wait for the counter trade you have less DD to deal with.

  * [#166](/thread/post/4925259#post4925259 "Post Permalink")

  * Edited 11:25pm  Sep 3, 2011 11:13pm | Edited 11:25pm 

  * [ jmw1970](jmw1970)

  * Joined Sep 2010 | Status: Trader & MQL Coder | [776 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=156350)

Dear All  
  
As promised here is a “Multi-pair” trader for the 1H CTR expert advisor.  
  
The logic is taken directly from the standard 1H CTR Both  
  
There are 2 slight modifications to the standard logic, they are as follows  
  
1) ECN brokers could not previously use the SL & TP from this EA, and Steve’s EA had to be used or the SL/TP added via MPTM, this version will allow any broker to use the SL/TP features  
2) The close on opposite band logic has been parametized, now the EA will only close on the opposite band if both of the following is true – the direction is set to Both, the Close on Opposite Band flag is set  
  
There is the ability to apply different magic numbers based on whether that pair is being used for range or for re-entry, if the currency pair is being used for Range (direction = both) then it will use the RangeMagicNbr, if the currency pair is being used for Re-Entry (direction = buy or sell) then it will use the ReEntryMagicNbr.  
  
Although by default I have set them both to 100 as I wasn’t exactly sure if this was needed.  
  
The EA uses several “buttons”, in all cases to “press” these pseudo “buttons” to change the state, highlight the “button” and drag it from its default position.  
  
The EA has 2 separate levels of control:-  
  
Main control – this is controlled by the “button” start/stop at the top of the screen, if the EA is stopped using this “button” then the EA will do absolutely nothing (mainly used if you need to change some parameters via F7) as the EA runs on a continuous loop and does not require ticks to run (apart from the first tick)  
  
Pair control – each pair can be individually controlled (the pair name is the “button”), if the pair is in red, then the EA will NOT perform any order management or entry processing (it will still show open orders & profit/loss). If the pair is in lime, then the EA will perform order management and entry processing.  
  
Each pair can be set up to trade in both directions, or buy / sell only, to change the direction “press” the direction “button”, it will cycle through in the following order (BOTH -> Buy -> Sell -> BOTH). For safety either ensure that the MA’s are within the Bollinger Bands (so no unexpected trades are opened) or use the pair control “button” to temporarily suspend the pair.  
  
By default the EA will start with ALL currency pairs temporarily suspended with a direction of BOTH.  
  
The current definition (UT,DT,BO,CTR) of the pairs "trend" is also displayed.  
  
If there is an open order, the order will be displayed along with it’s current Profit / Loss  
  
For the tinkerers around, the screen definition (placement of fields, font, colors etc) are setup in the “#define” section at the top of the EA. Changing the values here will automatically modify the screen setup.  
  
Refer to NB’s documentation on changing EA’s for assistance if required.  
  
Any questions, please do this via PM to avoid this thread being cluttered with technical queries not related to the method.  
  
Regards, John

  * [#169](/thread/post/4925589#post4925589 "Post Permalink")

  * Edited 9:30am  Sep 4, 2011 9:13am | Edited 9:30am 

  * [ jmw1970](jmw1970)

  * Joined Sep 2010 | Status: Trader & MQL Coder | [776 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=156350)

Hi  
  
I take it you mean something like recovery, although I am not an expert on this I thought recovery was handled by looking for the MA2 cross on the daily and using the recovery EA  
  
there is however two different work-arounds already coded into the EA to handle this  
  
Work Around 1  
a) temporarily suspend the pair (move the pair "button" so it is red)  
b) Create a global variable using F3 with a prefix = to the #define IgnorePfx, the default is "Z@Ignore #" after the # sign you put in the ticket number of the original trade (eg. Z@Ignore #123432250)  
c) if you have done this correctly the trade will now disappear from the dashboard  
d) when you think that the run is nearly over (or it has moved enough pips) stop the pair suspension (move the pair "button" so it is lime)  
e) the ea will then open a trade if the criteria is still met  
  
Work Around 2  
a) Ensure that you have 2 different magic numbers for the Range & Re-Entry  
b) Temporarily suspend the pair  
c) Change the direction from the one that created the original entry (so if originally was both and a buy order entered, change the direction to buy, if originally on buy and a buy order entered, change to both etc.)  
d) when you think that the run is nearly over (or it has moved enough pips) stop the pair suspension (move the pair "button" so it is lime)  
e) the ea will then open a trade if the criteria is still met  
  
not a perfect solution I know, but I was also looking at ways for the EA to ignore the fact that it already had an opened trade - but this would be in extra special circumstances and wasn't intended to be used on a regular basis  
  
Regards, John

Heck if I know here is the code if you want to double check your EA. Does anyone see something wrong??  
  
double Var1 = iBands(NULL, PERIOD_H4, 20, 1, 0, PRICE_CLOSE, MODE_UPPER, Current + 0);//PAIR, PERIOD, MA period, Deviation, shift  
double Var2 = iBands(NULL, PERIOD_H4, 20, 2, 0, PRICE_CLOSE, MODE_UPPER, Current + 0);  
double Var3 = iBands(NULL, PERIOD_H4, 20, 1, 0, PRICE_CLOSE, MODE_LOWER, Current + 0);  
double Var4 = iBands(NULL, PERIOD_H4, 20, 2, 0, PRICE_CLOSE, MODE_LOWER, Current + 0);  
double Var5 = iMA(NULL, PERIOD_H4, 3, 1, MODE_LWMA, PRICE_OPEN, Current + 0);  
  
  
if ( Var5 < Var3 && Bid < Var3 ) Order = SIGNAL_BUY;//VAR3 is the lower band  
if ( Var5 > Var1 && Bid > Var1 ) Order = SIGNAL_SELL;//Var1 is the upper band

  * Sep 11, 2011 4:54pm  Sep 11, 2011 4:54pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41648_3.gif) nanningbob](nanningbob)

  * Joined Jun 2007 | Status: Teach men to fish | [7,384 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41648)

> [Quoting Frodog](/thread/post/4944473#post4944473 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> Hi Bob, say you have a trade that goes 100 against you and then retraces 50 and hits the opposite bb, will you allow the ea to close the trade for a loss of 50 odd pips when it hits opposite bb, or will you shut the ea down and set a manual tp at be?
> 
> Ignored

The 1 Hour needs to be manually closed and I only use the BB close on the 4H first level. I will close a 2nd or 3rd level trade for profit and keep the 1 L loser to play with at a later date. I especially do this when I think price will range instead of giving a full retrace. So often my recovery trades are multiples instead of singles. On the other hand if I know I am just on the wrong end of a trade I will take anything close to a BE. So if I am 300 down at .2 lots and my .4 lot retraces 75 pips (other side of BB band) I will just take the acceptable loss especially if other trades that day make it even.

> Bob, would you recommend this course of action as per attached ea? I have this hedged and would need a 50 pip retrace to BE. Or I could just close the buy trade and enter a new sell off the ctr ea.

For me to even think I could get a 50 pip retrace on a EURO pair would be tough. A 50 pip loss is very acceptable with any Euro buy trade right now. You can sit on it until the Greek thing resolves itself or just take the loss. I would be hesitant to try to recover. At any moment Germany could say NO MORE and watch that thing drop like a rock, or Greece say NO MORE or France credit downgrade or ................... I think you get the picture. Anyone of those scenarios could drop the EURO very quickly. However, if I were to try such a thing I would do it during the jpy session where I have a very good chance that price would not run on me if it didn't succeed. If you had a BB bottom on a lower chart like 1H, 30M, etc and try to run it to the top during off hours would be the best bet.

  * [#190](/thread/post/4962518#post4962518 "Post Permalink")

  * Sep 17, 2011 8:21am  Sep 17, 2011 8:21am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41648_3.gif) nanningbob](nanningbob)

  * Joined Jun 2007 | Status: Teach men to fish | [7,384 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41648)

Despite sitting on 4 recovery trades for now NZD/CHF, CHF/JPY, GBP/USD and AUD/CAD I have been plugging along all month. It was definitely a slower week but still managed some profit. The problem with reporting is I trade all forms of my 10.0 system on one account. So I will report two numbers. All trades I increased my account since **Sept. 1 11.1%** The pairs just using the **1H CTR is 5.5%**. My win to loss ratio since Aug. 1 when I started using 10.0 for all my trading is **80.2%** which is over a 10% increase over my previous trading experience with my other systems from a 1 year period. So so far I am very pleased with the results both increase in my account and win to loss ratio. I also would note that I decreased my lot sizes a penny or two on trades with the breakout of the Greek/Euro stories last week. I wanted to be prepared for anything that could happen. So my results would have been higher if I had kept my same sizes but my DD would also have been bigger. dropping my lot sizes a tad allows me to keep my DD around the 10% figure. Almost all of that is involved in the 4 currencies mentioned above. I have done well shorting the EURO but my old habits of grabbing profit when it appears is limiting making a killing there but cant complain. 10.0 is working out very well. The big jump around the 70th trade was the gbp/chf trade I caught luckily. Cleared out some DD towards the end of the week by taking profit to clean out losses. I accidentally closed a trade I did not want to close for a loss. I accidentally closed the loss instead of the profit trade so I have that dip there.   
  
I have one piece of 10.0 left and that is the 4H system. I have been testing a different version of it and the results are far better than the one posted. One more week of testing a tweek I did yesterday on it and it will be ready to post. At that point the complete 10.0 series will be available. To my fellow 4H traders, I think it will be a killer system and is testing out to be the most profitable of the 10.0 trading systems. I will be calling it counter-trading back into the trend. It is mixing the sell high buy low system with 10.0 and CTR, so far it rocks. I am finding out that I am still a 4H counter trader at heart. It is still where I am most experienced at trading. ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1)

Here is my current g/c recovery. As you can see ctr took the 1st level right at the start of the DT. I then hedged at 100 pips. After PA steadied, I thought I would close the hedge and counter off the 1h ctr. As you can see PA decided to go downhill again...PA then touched the 2ma which indicated reversal or range time. At this point I decided to counter off the 4h ctr. PA then decided to go downhill again...So this is where I'm currently at. This got me thinking, maybe it would be better to just stick to 10.0 recovery instead of trying different methods of recovery ie. ctr 1 or 4h.

Bob,  
  
About the Nb 10.0 trading system EA, I brief summary like following table, please help to confirm my concept definition was right!  
and I found following another EA that I confused when time to adopt, please give me a guide.  
  
10.0 4H CTR BOTH B  
10.0 4H CTR BUY B  
10.0 4H CTR BUY B  
  
these EA logic major specific difference on :  
//+----------------------------------------------------+   
//| Signal Begin(Entry) |   
//+----------------------------------------------------+   
if ( Var5 < Var3 && Bid < Var3 ) Order = SIGNAL_BUY;  
if ( Var5 > Var1 && Bid > Var1 ) Order = SIGNAL_SELL;   
  
  
  
![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f61e.png?v=15.1)

>  ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f914.png?v=15.1)
> 
> Ignored

You wait until the low breaks the blue line when blue is above the red or the high breaks the blue line when blue is below the red line on the daily chart. That signals the run is over most of the time and it is safe to range trade, counter trade, or reversal of trend.   
  
If the fundamentals are strong these are the dips in an uptrend or a rally in a downtrend. For example the fundamentals are strong against the EURO right now so I wont do buys on it. So when the high breaks the blue I play a rally in a downtrend. So I will do sells on the Euro. I will continue to do this until the Euro settles on its debt issues.   
  
I wish I knew the fundamental on the pound right now other than it is being dragged down with the Euro. I have also settled on doing only sells on the pound also. Looks nice every 4-8 hours pocketing those profits. Still on the wrong side of the gbp/usd however.

>  Thanks
> 
> Ignored

In case Bob is busy I can answer this one. For NB systems you can use any template you like and or you can customize the existing templates. With some EAs which use a particular customized indicator then you need to have that indicator on your chart in order for the EAs to function properly. As far as I am aware non of Bob`s EAs need a customized indicator to function.  
  
Kind Regards

Since most of the trades are now in recovery I have spent most of my time in the 4H CT section. Doesnt mean I havent stopped range trading the 1H. Ok my trades and how they are going. Except for the AUD/NZD and USD/JPY. All the trades are in some form of recovery. I will list the pair, total negative pips all levels, when the 1L trade started and percentage of recovery so far since the 1L trade started. I also may make some comments on some of the pairs. It doesnt mean I have been losing all month I only am reporting since the trade went into recovery. My overall increase in my account for all 10.0 trades is 13.3%. Most of my recovery trades I am using the CT 4H system and some OI on the daily chart. Anyway here is range trading as of this weekend.   
  
aud/cad -310 since 9-9 recovered 57% so far. Not too worried about this pair since they are both commidity economies. If commodities go down they both will and this causes them to bounce around consistantly.   
  
aud/jpy -494 since 9-19 recovered 30%. China economy slowdown brings the aud down, BOJ desire to bring down the jpy. Let the bouncing begin.  
  
aud/nzd -75 this has been my best trading pair the last two months. Very reliable bouncing pair. Probably should just trade this and leave the rest.   
  
aud/usd -1637 9-9 recovered 18% Now that reports of Chinese economy in slow down and USD strengthening that is a double whammy. I am making this pair my #1 priority of getting out of. This trade is nothing but trouble right now. The one redeeming quality is China has been buying some AUD. So hopefully see a retrace and out. If you are not into this pair I would consider only sells on it for now.   
  
cad/jpy -629 9-19 recovered 11% I am expecting BOJ to step in at some point and stop the jpy from further strengthening. Will wait this one out.

USD/JPY I will only do buys with this pair for now. JPY wants to weaken its currency and the USD is on a strong move. SO why fight it. Do buys in the dips.

  * Oct 8, 2011 6:57am  Oct 8, 2011 6:57am 

  * [ Frodog](frodog)

  * | Joined Jun 2009  | Status: Trader | [104 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=106966)

Hi Starlogic,  
I was trading the same pairs as Bob (low volatile) Things have gone really downhill for me. I traded my account from $2500 up to $3600 over 3 or 4 months trading .02 standard lots. BUT....after the recent trending my account took a fatal hit... my equity is now at about $300 ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f641.png?v=15.1) I found that because most pairs are so correlated they almost all move in the same direction. A couple of key things I learnt from this is:  
  
.02 standard lots for my account size was too big for the amount of pairs I was trading (12 pairs)   
  
DO NOT let your account go over 20%DD. Close out trades when this happens, so DD comes back down.  
  
At the moment my balance is $1300 so i'm just going to recover these last trades I have and then probably withdraw my $$ 

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

Here i bragged about you to others. The dd hits do come in range trading it is just how you deal with it. Since I trade small I get through these patches. Like I said in my recovery I used about half of my Sept. profit to take out some trades. Things are under control for now. If there is another run I do have some room again. To me if 10.0 Range trading survives these moves then I think I finally found a range system that works just using an EA and you interfere with recovery. Anyway it appears that 1 penny per 500 of account seems to be a safe number to trade with. I only went over 20% of my account because of trades outside this system. The chf/jpy is going to take some time to recover but the rest are very doable. Good luck.

  * [#223](/thread/post/5023180#post5023180 "Post Permalink")

  * Oct 8, 2011 7:22pm  Oct 8, 2011 7:22pm 

  * [ censura](censura)

  * | Joined Sep 2006  | Status: Trader | [405 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=17875)

The secret to this range system is the dd control which i know is stating the obvious. You will always have winners from this system but the trick is to make sure the runs dont kill you.  
  
I introduced sometime ago my hedge at 100 system it has saved me and i have continued to post gains throught the two months (since aug 12th) i posted results for a while but stopped as i felt it had no use apart from my ego. Since Aug 12th my account has grown by 187% my drawdown has never been over 24% (This was when i did not catch the hedge in time as it is not a auto (still awating this via phover new panel)  
  
I have evolved my system as before i hedged and either matched lossers with winners as and when (the best method as it frees up those pairs to trade again- the issue with hedging is obviously it takes those pairs out of the game)  
  
Now if the pair looks like a bb runner and using other indicators related to volume spread analysis (VSA) i place my second trade with the trend - i am also considering doing this automatically. or if it is seperated from the bb then i await the retrace using the recovery ea  
  
I never compound my trades ie using the traditional 1,1,2,4 or other lot increase , i understand it but effectivley each trade is still a risk and if it goes against me i am further in the do do . So i stick to my base lot size. Also if i have not enough winners to offset then i generally wait and will pick off trades 1 at a time controlling my dd using some fundemenatals as a guide. It is not set and forgett so it has a lot of descretion in it. My point is (and i borrowed this from another thred basket trading) i see it as a business with stock controll, cashflow and profit/loss and if i have say 9 or 10 in hedge (which has happened ) i am not going to get the sam volume of winners so it can take time to match them out and take decsions 1 at a time - occassionally i will wipe the slate clean particualrly friday at 4-30 uk time and start again at 5am UK time (alot of my losses have happened sunday/monday so i have stopped trading at these times. Also i will stopp/ hedge everything if real major news is coming and wait till things settle. (This is range trading and i dont want to be the wrong side of a currency going of on a big run particualrly if i am not watching to hedge)  
  
So just thought i would add my 2 penny worth this dd mng is a study in its own right and i think it will take me sometime to get to grips with it but nb has given me a platform and though process. The best tactic for me is the hedge means each pair is never to far out to put you in problems especially if you are patience and here is another key- you can trade all your life , every weekday is a trading day, but your account need protecting it is your lifeline and the mkt does not care about it so you must.  
  
take care

  * Oct 10, 2011 10:38am  Oct 10, 2011 10:38am 

  * [ yonnie](yonnie)

  * Joined May 2008 | Status: Trader | [1,158 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=69076)

censura,  
  
you hedge at -100 pips: what is the rush to close out these 2 trades - price might come back to -50 in a couple of days/weeks and you close out the trades without a loss.  
in the meantime your loss wont get any larger than -100 on the 2 trades anyway.  
  
when hedged you say you cannot trade in that pair: why not, after all that trade is hedged?  
  
just trying to understand and thank you for your reply![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1)

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

  * [#228](/thread/post/5025116#post5025116 "Post Permalink")

  * Oct 10, 2011 10:42am  Oct 10, 2011 10:42am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41648_3.gif) nanningbob](nanningbob)

  * Joined Jun 2007 | Status: Teach men to fish | [7,384 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41648)

When you want to undo a hedge wait until the 10.0 system gives you the ranging period and then take out one hedge at the high and the other at the low. This way you are out with out a loss.

The purpose of a hedge is to stop time. The trade that was going against you is stopped in time until you get a market in your favor. It is an account saver if a sudden story comes. I was furious that they stopped hedging in the USA. That was my backup plan to a super bad trade. Now I use smaller lots so I can use a bigger ranger in trading. I always know a market I like will eventually happen.

Digging myself out of a hole here but getting out. I am glad I down sized my lot size at the end of September or I would have had to add funds. Not because of the pairs here but some other trades I took.  
  
Anyway, still in recovery _aud/cad, aud/jpy, chf/jpy, cad/jap, gbp/usd, nzd/jpy, usd/cad_  
  
Most of them I am close to clearing out. Some are reduced in lot sizes so they are not that deep money wise anymore.   
  
These pairs I am back to normal trading with the Range EA  
  
aud/nzd (probably the best pair to trade)  
aud/usd this one I just took some losses on cleaned out 1st and 2nd levels last week. Could have hung in there but I didnt want to violate my 20% rule. When over 20% DD start clearing out trades or add funds. Then next DD I experience I may make a new rule where if I go over 15% DD all profits must be used to clear DD. I have a tendency to keep pocking profits and letting DD get bigger. If I had done that with a couple of trades I might not have had to close any big losers. Any way will try that one. I have dropped aud/usd from my list, I think pairing that small of a pair with a major like USD will always lead to trouble some where.  
_eur/gb_ p this one held steady all the way through.  
_gbp/ca_ d another good customer with some exciting moments at times.  
_nzd/chf_ DANG SNB still it came back and cleaned itself out.  
_usd/jpy_ wish this one would move just a little more.  
  
The range pairs did as advertised stayed within a range during a big run. CHF bank interference made it more exciting than it should be.

Bob,  
  
It seems to me the single most important question you can ask before you take a trade is "Is this a trending or a ranging market". If it is a ranging market you should make one trade. And if it is a trending market you should the opposite.   
  
How do you decide which is which?

> Ignored

Definition of a range trade is when the Low or high is touching any of the two lines on the daily chart. Price is trending when the low and high are not touching any of the lines on a daily chart.

> [Quoting nanningbob](/thread/post/4868659#post4868659 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> One last thing about recovery trades. Recovery trades and negative DD are simple interest trades. In other words they happen once and they are done, no compounding. Winning trades are compound interest. In other words profits continue to increase the account and each winning trade is like banking compound interest over a long period of time. Losing trades and DD are simple interest in that once they are done they no long continue to add to the loses. So as my DD grew and diminished in size, my winners kept increasing my account like compound interest...
> 
> Ignored

Bob,   
  
I am going through your past posts, finding things I see as interesting, and commenting on them. I hope you don't mind. Let me know if this starts to clog things up.  
  
I see your method as very similar to that of the business model of a clothing store. You buy your clothes, put them out for sale. You only sell when you have a profit and since you are not using a stoploss, you never sell for a loss.  
  
At seasons end you have accumulated "Junk" inventory. You dump this at a loss and move onto the next season of clothing. This system works because the net profit during peak season counteracts losses from the season end sales.  
  
With this metaphor, your DD is really the cost of maintaining a stock of goods in your store.   
  
I find the metaphor of interest does not work that well for me because for me the central fact of interest is not that it increases your balance, but that it makes your account grow in geometrically.

> Thank you for your note. I dont know why but FOREX seems to be a different animal when it comes to trading rules. I finally believed them to be mostly garbage.   
> 
> 
> Ignored

Well said.   
  
the one central difference between the forex market and all other markets is the extreme leverage that is being used. This leverage really benefits two people.   
  
1\. the broker. a 2 pip commission at 100:1 leverage means 100X profit.  
2\. bankers. Bankers need liquidity to function. If retail traders go out there with 1:1 leverage the volume would be so small that it would make no difference to them. Also, with low leverage, forex is no where near as exciting. And that would also reduce the number of players. Double whammy.
